The formula for CAGR is:\n   CAGR = ( (Ending Value / Beginning Value)^(1 / Number of Years) ) - 1\n   Where:\n   - Ending Value: GDP in 2024\n   - Beginning Value: GDP in 2000\n   - Number of Years: 2024 - 2000 = 24 years.\n3. **Projection:** Project the GDP for 2049 by applying the calculated CAGR to the 2024 GDP figure. The formula for projection would be:\n   Projected GDP in 2049 = GDP in 2024 * (1 + CAGR)^(2049 - 2024)\n   Projected GDP in 2049 = GDP in 2024 * (1 + CAGR)^25\n\n**Reasoning:**\nThis method assumes that the historical growth trend observed between 2000 and 2024 will continue into the future until 2049. While this is a simplification and actual GDP growth can be influenced by various unpredictable factors (e.g., technological advancements, geopolitical events, economic crises, policy changes), it provides a baseline projection based on past performance.
